2025-06-01T02:40:24.6869390Z         (for example by using `find_namespace_packages(...)`/`find_namespace:`
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6869520Z         instead of `find_packages(...)`/`find:`).
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6869570Z 
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6869910Z         You can read more about "package discovery" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6869980Z 
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6870190Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/package_discovery.html
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6870240Z 
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6870440Z         If you don't want 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' to be distributed and are
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6870630Z         already explicitly excluding 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' via
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6870910Z         `find_namespace_packages(...)/find_namespace` or `find_packages(...)/find`,
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6871190Z         you can try to use `exclude_package_data`, or `include-package-data=False` in
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6871380Z         combination with a more fine grained `package-data` configuration.
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6871430Z 
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6871630Z         You can read more about "package data files" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6871680Z 
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6871860Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/datafiles.html
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6873450Z 
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6873850Z 
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6874430Z         [^1]: For Python, any directory (with suitable naming) can be imported,
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6874910Z               even if it does not contain any `.py` files.
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6875110Z               On the other hand, currently there is no concept of package data
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6875290Z               directory, all directories are treated like packages.
2025-06-01T02:40:24.6875420Z         ********************************************************************************
